  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>I run Hadoop-0.20 on distributed mode on 10 VMs (NameNode + JobTracker + 8 DataNodes/TaskTrackers) with Mahout trunk.<br> I tried to test kmeans example with build-reuters.sh but I got an IndexOutOfBoundException when it starts kmeans.<br> I don't know which operation fails ... ExtractReuters, seqdirectory, seq2sparse or kmeans. Maybe I forgot a configuration ? I searched on the web and didn't find solutions ... </p> 
                  <p>------------------------ UPDATE == 05/16 -------------------------</p> 
                  <p>NameNode:/usr/local/mahout/trunk/examples/bin# ./build-reuters.sh <br> Please select a number to choose the corresponding clustering algorithm<br> 1. kmeans clustering<br> 2. lda clustering<br> Enter your choice : 1<br> ok. You chose 1 and we'll use kmeans Clustering<br> ./build-reuters.sh: line 39: cd: examples/bin/: No such file or directory<br> Downloading Reuters-21578<br> % Total % Received % Xferd Average Speed Time Time Time Current<br> Dload Upload Total Spent Left Speed<br> 100 7959k 100 7959k 0 0 121k 0 0:01:05 0:01:05 -<del>:</del><del>:</del>- 99k<br> Extracting...<br> Running on hadoop, using HADOOP_HOME=/usr/lib/hadoop-0.20<br> No HADOOP_CONF_DIR set, using /usr/lib/hadoop-0.20/src/conf <br> 11/05/16 09:31:20 WARN driver.MahoutDriver: No With the latest version of Lucene, ExtractReuters it appends -tmp on to the directory name, hence the message \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ctt\u003eDeleting all files in .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/-tmp\u003c\\/tt\u003e\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe next step in build-reuters.sh is to run seqdirectory on .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out, which ends up producing an empty sequence file. You can confirm this by doing:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ctt\u003e.\\/bin\\/mahout seqdumper -s examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out-seqdir\\/chunk-0\u003c\\/tt\u003e\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe result should indicate that this file is empty. The problem isn\'t caught until the k-means clusterer tries to grab random vectors out of the sequence files generated by seq2sparse, which of course is also empty.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eTo workaround, try:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ctt\u003emv .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/-tmp\\/* .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/ &amp;&amp; rmdir .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/-tmp\u003c\\/tt\u003e\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAnd re-run build-reuters.sh - it should work this time around.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThis didn\'t fail for me initially because I still had a .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out directory containing the dataset around from a previous run.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAs an aside, instead of editing your original message, just post the additional details in a follow-up comment. The way JIRA works, it is much easier to track the status of the ticket that way.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"drew.farris\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13035925_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=drew.farris\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"drew.farris\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Drew Farris\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13035925_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'19\\/May\\/11 01:48\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-05-19T01:48:09+0000\'\u003e19\\/May\\/11 01:48\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Allan, \\n\\n It appears that the problem is due to a change in the behavior of the org.apache.lucene.benchmark.utils.ExtractReuters utility from Lucene that is executed as a part of build-reuters.sh.  \\n\\n Prior to Lucene 3.1.0 it would extract the Reuters data to the specified output directory, in this case .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out. With the latest version of Lucene, ExtractReuters it appends -tmp on to the directory name, hence the message  \\n\\n  Deleting all files in .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/-tmp  \\n\\n The next step in build-reuters.sh is to run seqdirectory on .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out, which ends up producing an empty sequence file. You can confirm this by doing: \\n\\n  .\\/bin\\/mahout seqdumper -s examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out-seqdir\\/chunk-0  \\n\\n The result should indicate that this file is empty. The problem isn\'t caught until the k-means clusterer tries to grab random vectors out of the sequence files generated by seq2sparse, which of course is also empty. \\n\\n To workaround, try: \\n\\n  mv .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/-tmp\\/* .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/ &amp;&amp; rmdir .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out\\/-tmp  \\n\\n And re-run build-reuters.sh - it should work this time around. \\n\\n This didn\'t fail for me initially because I still had a .\\/examples\\/bin\\/work\\/reuters-out directory containing the dataset around from a previous run. \\n\\n As an aside, instead of editing your original message, just post the additional details in a follow-up comment. \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eUpdated build-reuters.sh to be a bit more sane about its working directory, sensitive to whether mahout will execute in local or distributed mode and to reuse the reuters-reuters-sgm, reuters-out and reuters-out-seqdir directories if they already exist.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWork is done in a directory called mahout-work, seqdirectory is always run locally, and if in distributed mode, the result are copied up to hdfs. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAlso updated output of lda and kmeans so that their directory names do not overlap.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThis could do a better job of cleaning up before\\/after it executes, but it gets the job done.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ePlease take a look and give this a try, I\'ve run kmeans in local and distributed mode (forcing local by unsetting HADOOP_HOME), I am running lda in distributed mode now, but my cluster is small and it takes a long time to complete. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Drew Farris\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13037404_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'21\\/May\\/11 15:18\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-05-21T15:18:27+0000\'\u003e21\\/May\\/11 15:18\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Updated build-reuters.sh to be a bit more sane about its working directory, sensitive to whether mahout will execute in local or distributed mode and to reuse the reuters-reuters-sgm, reuters-out and reuters-out-seqdir directories if they already exist. \\n\\n Work is done in a directory called mahout-work, seqdirectory is always run locally, and if in distributed mode, the result are copied up to hdfs.  \\n\\n Also updated output of lda and kmeans so that their directory names do not overlap. \\n\\n This could do a better job of cleaning up before\\/after it executes, but it gets the job done. \\n\\n Please take a look and give this a try, I\'ve run kmeans in local and distributed mode (forcing local by unsetting HADOOP_HOME), I am running lda in distributed mode now, but my cluster is small and it takes a long time to complete.  \\n             \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n
